Vishnu Kumar N.D a Male Child born to N.R. Dhamotharan on 22-10-1990 residing at No. 4/82, Sourasthrapuram
4th Street, Vandiyur, Madurai-625 020, Has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
by Dr. V. Jayaraman Ms, MCh, MNAMS, Dip. N.B., Phd., FICS. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth
be known as Vishnu Priya N.D
Madurai,
1st March 2016.

VISHNU KUMAR, N.D.
